name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Basic Single Room
info:Stayed in November 2021
info:Business travelers
info:1 Review
rating:2.5
posted:Posted November 22, 2021
msg:Location is good, near subway number 5. Room was quite clean but old.
Me and my chinese wife did the trip when it was required a swab to enter Chongqing if arriving from Chengdu. We did the swab in Chengdu as required and crossed the checkpoint at train station without any problem. Once arrived at hotel they pretend we do another swab at our expenses, because that was the "local rules". My wife ask who set such "local rule", no clear answer obtained. After a bit of discussions we went to our business, saying that we were available to do another swab at their expenses and when we were free, because such rule wasn't coming from the Government. Once more, no answer, but as result the staff woke up us at 2 o'clock in the night ringing the bell at door with the excuse "we asked for a USB charger". It was clearly an excuse because USB chargers and cables are already available in the room if necessary (you have to pay, but are there).
We left one day in advance although the night wasn't refundable.
